INTERNATIONAL STUDIES 
GERMAN PROTESTANTS FACE THE SOCIAL QUESTION, by William O. Shanahan. By bringing about a massive reorganization of the traditional agrarian world the Industrial Revolution so altered man’s work, his home, and his habits of thought as to place Christianity in jeopardy. The German Protestants became entangled with the national political history in attempting to deal with the social question. How their attempts entered into German history after 1815 provides the narrative of this book. And throughout, the historian’s interest in depicting the ties between Christianity and western culture has not been lost to sight. In this dimension, the story of the German Protestant response to the Industrial Revolu­tion illumines the fate of western man. 
$6.75 
PAN-SLAVISM: ITS HISTORY AND IDEOLOGY, by Hans Kohn. A scholar brought up in Prague, the center of the Pan-Slavist movement of the 19th cen­tury, writes on a question so necessary to the understanding of the complex problems which the emergence of the Slav nations, above all Russia, to full political and cultural participation in the life of the 19th and 20th centuries created for them, for the other peoples, and for Western civilization. 
$6.25 
DIPLOMACY IN A WHIRLPOOL: HUNGARY BETWEEN NAZI GERMANY AND SOVIET RUSSIA, by Stephen D. Kertesz. A concise and well written study of the Soviet pentration and domination of Hungry, presented by a man who served in the Hungarian diplomatic service during and after the war. 
$4-75 
SOVIET IMPERIALISM: ITS ORIGINS AND TACTICS, edited by Waldemar Gurian. A basic survey of Soviet expansionism by N. Timasheff of Fordham, Michael Pap of Notre Dame, W. Weintraub of Harvard, R. Pipes of Harvard, F. Barghoom of Yale, and Ling Nai-jui of Notre Dame. 
$3-75 
THE FOREIGN POLICY OF THE BRITISH LABOUR GOVERNMENT: 1945­1951, by M. A. Fitzsimons. An analysis of Labour’s foreign policy aspirations and performance. 
$3 25 
BOLSHEVISM: AN INTRODUCTION TO SOVIET COMMUNISM, by Walde­mar Gurian. A clear and cogent treatment of the realities of Russian Communism and its appeal as a secular religion. 
$3-25 
CHRISTIAN DEMOCRACY IN ITALY AND FRANCE, by Mario Einaudi and Francois Goguel. A study of the Christian Democratic Party in Italy and the MRP, the party of the Fourth French Republic. 
$400 
EUROPE BETWEEN DEMOCRACY AND ANARCHY, by F. A. Hermens. An important volume on the effects of Proportional Representation between 1918 and iQKO. 
$4.00 
University of Notre Dame Press 
Notre Dame, Indiana
